 supreme court main raashtragan ko lekar aham sunwaayee hui
 Last November 30, the Supreme Court had said in an important interim order related to the national anthem, 'jana Gana Mana', that the national anthem would be played before the film started in all theaters across the country
 supreme court ne yah bhi kaha ki raashtragan bajte samay cinemahol ke parde par rashtriya dhvaj dikhaaya janaa bhi anivaary hoga, tathaa cinemaghar main maujuud sabhi logon ko raashtragan ke sammaan main khadaa hona hoga
 The Supreme Court held that the national anthem is associated with national identity, national unity and constitutional patriotism
 court ke aadesh ke mutabik, dhyaan rakhaa jaae ki kisi bhi vyavsaayik hit main raashtragan kaa istemaal nahin kiya ja saktaa
 Apart from this, the national anthem will not be used to create drama in any kind of activity, and the national anthem will not be sung as Variety Song either
 darasal, shyaam narayan chaukase kii yachika main kaha gaya tha ki kisi bhi vyavsaayik gatividhi ke liye raashtragan ke chalan par roak lagaai jaani chahie, or antertenment sho main drama creat karne ke liye raashtragan ko istemaal na kiya jaae
 The petition also stated that once started the national anthem should be sung to the end, and not stopped in between
 yachika main court se yah aadesh dene kaa aagrah bhi kiya gaya tha ki raashtragan ko aise logon ke bich na gaaya jaae, jo ise nahin samajhate

 yachika main kaha gaya ki is tarah ke maamalon main raashtragan niyamon kaa ulanghan he or yah varsh 1971 ke kanoon ke khilaaf he
 Earlier, the Supreme Court, hearing this petition, issued a notice to the Central Government seeking an answer
 tippaniyan The Supreme Court had said that when people respect the national anthem and the national flag, it will inculcate the spirit of patriotism and nationalism in the minds of the people
 supreme court ne kaha ki ye logon kii fundamental duty he ki vah samvidhan kaa aadar karen or uskaa paalan karen or phir sanvaidhanik sansthaanon, raashtragan or rashtriya dhvaj kaa sammaan karen
 The bench of Supreme Court Justice Deepak Mishra also said that it is clear that it is the duty of all citizens to follow the ideals of the Constitution
 adaalat ne kaha tha ki samay kii maang he ki desh ke naagarik mahasoos karen ki vah desh main rahete hai or unki duty he ki vah raashtragan kaa sammaan karen jo ki sanvaidhanik deshbhakti or rashtriyata kaa pratik he
 Freedom in this matter cannot be given in the name of personal thinking
 yaheen kisi vyaktigat soch kii jagah nahin he
 This is not acceptable under the constitutional model
 vahiin, supreme court main is aadesh ko lekar daakhil yachikaaon main kaha gaya he ki is aadesh ko waapas len kyonki ye aadesh adhikaron kaa hanan karte hai

 is maamle kii agali sunwaayee 18 april ko hogi
 The Supreme Court held a major hearing on the national anthem
 pichley 30 november ko supreme court ne raashtragan, yani 'jan gana man' se jude ek ahm antarim aadesh main kaha tha ki deshbhar ke sabhi cinemagharon main film shuru hone se pehle raashtragan bajegaa
 The Supreme Court also said that it would be mandatory to show the national flag on the screen of the cinema hall while playing the national anthem, and all those present in the cinema hall would have to stand in honor of the national anthem
 supreme court ne kaha ki raashtragan rashtriya pahchaan, rashtriya ekta or sanvaidhanik deshbhakti se judaa he
 According to the court order, it should be kept in mind that the national anthem cannot be used in any commercial interest
 iske alaava kisi bhi tarah kii gatividhi main drama creat karne ke liye bhi raashtragan kaa istemaal nahin hoga, tathaa raashtragan ko vairieti song ke taur par bhi nahin gaaya jayega
 In fact, the petition by Shyam Narayan Chokse said that the practice of the national anthem should be banned for any commercial activity, and that the national anthem should not be used to create drama in entertainment shows
 yachika main yah bhi kaha gaya tha ki ek baar shuru hone par raashtragan ko ant tak gaaya janaa chahie, or bich main band nahin kiya janaa chahie
 The petition also urged the court to order that the national anthem should not be sung among people who do not understand it
 iske atirikt raashtragan kii dhun badalakar kisi ore tareeke se gane kii ijazat nahin milani chahie
 The petition said that in such cases the national anthem is in violation of the rules and it is against the 1971 law
 isse pehle, supreme court ne is yachika par sunwaayee karte hue centre sarkaar ko notice jari kar jawaab maanga tha
 The comments supreme court ne kaha tha ki jab log raashtragan or rashtriya dhvaj kaa aadar karenge to isse logon ke man main deshbhakti or rashtrawaad kii bhaavana jagegi
 The Supreme Court said that it is the fundamental duty of these people to respect and follow the constitution and then to honor constitutional institutions, the national anthem and the national flag
 supreme court ke justise deepak mishra kii bench ne ye bhi kaha tha ki ye baat saaf he ki sabhi nagarikon kaa daayitv he ki vah samvidhan ke adarsh ko maane

 vah subah team hotel main kek kaatenge
 Mumbai Indians team manager said, "we have a special program in the morning before the match, in which Tendulkar will cut the cake and talk in front of the media
" tendulkar kii patni anjali or mumbai team kii maalik nita ambani aaj raat yahaan pahunch rahi hai

" unhen party karnaa pasand nahin he or is baar bhi aisa hi hoga

 cab adhyaksh jagmohan daalamia ne kaha, cab tab bhi jashn manaanaa chahega jab vah 100 saal ke ho jaaenge

 chocolate, kek, ghana or madagascar se mangavaaye gaye khaas cocao se taiyaar kiya jayega

 We are proud of it
 kek par tendulkar kii ek tasviir hogi jo 2 april 2011 ko mili vishwacap jeet ke baad kii tasviir he

 pichley saal cab ne donon tiimon ke ipel mukaable ke dauraan tendulkar ko sau antarrashtriya shatak ke liye sau ginniyaan dekar sammanit kiya tha

 tippaniyan In his 24-year career, Tendulkar has captured almost all records except Brian Lara's unbeaten 400 in Test cricket
 van-de cricket ko alavida kah chuke tendulkar ne 463 maichon main 49 shatak samet 18426 ran banaae hai
